  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_c7c6e8c7-a1a0-42db-a372-ebc12a0af058'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

<div id="review_346590084" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/346590084" />
    <a title="♡Karlyn P♡" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1131400-karlyn-p"><img alt="♡Karlyn P♡" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1389996373p2/1131400.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/346590084?book_show_action=true">Jun 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♡Karlyn P♡" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♡Karlyn P♡" href="/user/show/1131400-karlyn-p">♡Karlyn P♡</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=published-2012">published-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=genre-contemporary">genre-contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=steam-hot">steam-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=genre-humor">genre-humor</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=funny">funny</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer346590084" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6842942811821010705"><br/><b>Yes!!! Another Neighbor From Hell!!</b><br/><br/>If you want to read about a knight-in-shining armor type hero, a kind and handsome man with sparkling bright teeth who always says the perfect thing and rescues his damsel in distress to save the day -- then don't read this book. Seriously!<br/><br/>Why? Because RL Mathewson tosses that cliche stereotypical romance formula out the window! What you get in the Neighbor From Hell series is a very different kind of hero: a hot guy with (most likely) food in his teeth, who sa</span>
  <span id="freeText6842942811821010705" style="display:none"><br /><b>Yes!!! Another Neighbor From Hell!!</b><br /><br />If you want to read about a knight-in-shining armor type hero, a kind and handsome man with sparkling bright teeth who always says the perfect thing and rescues his damsel in distress to save the day -- then don't read this book. Seriously!<br /><br />Why? Because RL Mathewson tosses that cliche stereotypical romance formula out the window! What you get in the Neighbor From Hell series is a very different kind of hero: a hot guy with (most likely) food in his teeth, who says some of the most obnoxious stuff, and is very likely to be the person stressing out the damsel - not the one rescuing her! These stories are a riot! And best of all, she makes me a believer in these heroes. Oh yes, I love this series. <br /><br />Rory and Connor have been at each others throats since childhood, and are the bane to each others existence. School administrators separated their classes, stores and restaurants have either banned them or wont allow them in together, and they've even spent time in jail a time or two when their feuding goes too far. Their reputation around town is notorious. But they are also very much alike, so if only they'd quit fighting long enough to recognize it they might finally see what is fueling all those sparks between them.<br /><br />In CHECKMATE Connor and Rory are bidding on the same construction project, and find themselves having to work together. Connor and Rory soon battle for control, and working together turns out just as expected - a disaster! <br /><br />Connor and Rory are also - you guessed it - next door neighbors. While Connor may tell everyone he bought the house next to Rory because he planned to fix it up and sell it, and tormenting her is a nice bonus, the truth is he can't be away from her. He has secretly protected her over the years from awful boyfriends, and the event in Canada (I wont spoil it!) reveals much about his true feelings. <br /><br />Rory is just as attracted to Connor, but she tells herself it is only a physical attraction since he is such a hot guy. Nothing will come of it. But when Connor blackmails Rory into pretending to be his doting, loving girlfriend (who must hang on his every word!) in order for her to get control of a special project he snagged from her, the game is ON. And both plan to win what they want.<br /><br />The chemistry between Connor and Rory heat up to SMOKING. I really enjoyed these enemies-to-lovers. And we get to see our favorite Bradfords too!! Jason and Trevor, and their wives, make several appearances. Turns out Rory is cousins to the Bradford clan. <br /><br />The story has an emotional punch too. As expected it is hilarious, steamy and frustrating (in a good way!), but the story includes a secondary character struggling. It had me crying at one point, and I didn't see that coming. <br /><br />Rory has five older brothers, all single, who work for her on the construction crew. I assume these guys may be heroes in later books, hard to say. We meet a few new Bradfords too (including twins!). I wasn't all the impressed with Rory's brothers, they were all interchangeable mean bullies, IMO. Maybe they can be redeemed, but there was one scene toward the end that made me really not like them. SPOILER: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Two brothers hold someone down by the arms, while a third brother punches on him. That kind of fighting is just cowardly and dirty, so I was not liking them at all by that point. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br />The ending is very typical Mathewson, and I was hooting and laughing my way through this entire book. There were some moments at the end where I wish certain things might have happened a bit differently, and some things said differently, but they are my own nits. CHECKMATE was another great over-the-top romance farce by RL Mathewson. It kept me laughing, and I can't wait to read what's next in this series. <br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6842942811821010705" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_467351342" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/467351342" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/467351342?book_show_action=true">Nov 30, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of lighthearted contemporary romance</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Stacia (the 2010 club) by: </span>
      Buddy reading for the tREEoLA collective joint review effort
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer467351342" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16821476188145519849"><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/449054176' rel='nofollow noopener'>Check out my collective review with friends for tREEoLA here!</a><br/><br/><b>
  <blockquote>
    <u>A Story of Hot Chocolate</u>
    <br/>
    <br/>
    <i>You can drink it in your car<br/>You can drink it at a bar<br/>You can drink it in a chair<br/>You don't even have to share<br/>You can have it with some cream<br/>It is sure to make you gleam<br/>You can smell it from afar<br/>Be sure to store it in a jar<br/>But for the love of all that's holy<br/>Don't you dare steal it from Rory</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br/>Believe it or not, that was an actual summary of the book. I think I read more about one woman's lo</span>
  <span id="freeText16821476188145519849" style="display:none"><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/449054176" rel="nofollow noopener">Check out my collective review with friends for tREEoLA here!</a><br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>
    <u>A Story of Hot Chocolate</u>
    <br />
    <br />
    <i>You can drink it in your car<br />You can drink it at a bar<br />You can drink it in a chair<br />You don't even have to share<br />You can have it with some cream<br />It is sure to make you gleam<br />You can smell it from afar<br />Be sure to store it in a jar<br />But for the love of all that's holy<br />Don't you dare steal it from Rory</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br />Believe it or not, that was an actual summary of the book. I think I read more about one woman's love of hot chocolate/cocoa than I did anything else. I should have thought to look up how many times the word cocoa was used. <br /><br /><i>Checkmate</i> was decent enough, but I didn't feel the same magical spark that I experienced while reading the first <i>Neighbor From Hell</i> installment. All of the same components were there...we had humor, torture, sexual tension, etc. For all of that, I did enjoy the story. Maybe I just fell in love with Jason and Hayley's personalities from the first book so much more. Connor from this book did win me over in the end after I found out why he did some of the things that he did, but wow, he sure came across as annoyingly chauvinistic for a while. It does count with me that the person changed eventually, so I'm not knocking him...I just didn't warm up to him as easily as I did with Jason because Jason had that fun and crazy vibe which Connor was lacking.<br /><br />Story wise, we had a little hiccup going on between the 20-40% mark. It took me well over a week to get the motivation to delve back into the story after it stalled out. <i>However, I am glad that I did.</i> Once the chemistry kicked in, I truly enjoyed the rest of my time reading. <br /><br /><b>Strong points :</b><br /><br />Humor - I laughed at some of the stunts Connor pulled when he was terrorizing Rory.<br /><br />Sexual tension - I never thought I'd enjoy reading so many kissing scenes back-to-back. For some reason, it never got repetitive to me. I found the lead-up to the actual sex scenes to be just as fun as anything else. <br /><br /><b>Weak points :</b><br /><br />The construction story was boring - I would have preferred another vehicle to bring these two together.<br /><br />The hot cocoa ridiculousness - This should have been mentioned no more than 5 times max. This habit of Rory's was a setup for something that came later in the story, but I still would have gotten what Connor was trying to do, even with far fewer mentions of cocoa.<br /><br />There were a few minor spelling issues...but only a few.<br /><br /><b>Overall, this was still a fun and sexy read</b> There was nothing new or ground-breaking going on, but I'd rank this <i>just slightly</i> above average for a contemporary romance.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16821476188145519849" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer445439908" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14940629706498630071">Connor the hero, was a bully. Right from a kid pulling on Rory, the h's pigtails until the current time. He laced her food with laxatives when they were a teenager! He routinely steals her hot cocoa in the morning because *she* likes it. WTH?! Seriously, his bullying over 20+ years is painful to read. I can't imagine why or how Rory and her family and any SANE person put up with it. Underneath, it was love? Oh please, time honored excuse doesn't make it right. She should have gotten a restrainin</span>
  <span id="freeText14940629706498630071" style="display:none">Connor the hero, was a bully. Right from a kid pulling on Rory, the h's pigtails until the current time. He laced her food with laxatives when they were a teenager! He routinely steals her hot cocoa in the morning because *she* likes it. WTH?! Seriously, his bullying over 20+ years is painful to read. I can't imagine why or how Rory and her family and any SANE person put up with it. Underneath, it was love? Oh please, time honored excuse doesn't make it right. She should have gotten a restraining order on him! Connor himself acknowledges this and I think it's supposed to connect us to the hero?Connor almost crossed into stalker territory a number of times. And then blackmail trope. <br /><br />So, I think the author maybe tried to take a number of tropes and work it differently. But she failed. Spectacularly. The tomboyish daughter with over-protective 5 older brothers vying for approval and love from her father (but who thinks the world revolves around her) fails. The tomboyish h is yearning for someone to treat her as a girl and only Connor sees it. The blackmail trope where the hero has a nefarious intention behind also didn't work. Connor recovers well before their "bargain end-date" and voids their supposed agreement without revealing his intentions. And when this intention becomes clear in the <b>last</b> chapter, we are supposed to see the trust etc between them. But no, it was very clumsy execution that I didn't really see the point in that chapter. In fact, I felt that the author lost track of the motives halfway into the book. Everything meandered and towards the end, most of the situation was fairly pointless. Seriously, if the characters talked, it would have solved most of the problems.<br /><br />At the end, it was Connor who let the book. The author took him too far a bully that it was really hard for her to convince me that Connor and Rory belonged. Even though in the book, Rory is shown to be fighting back, I can't think of her except as a victim. 3 days into them "going-out" he manages to make her bail on her customary night out with her brothers which he has been going regularly for the past 10 years. That screams controlling to me. So yeah, at the end, I felt for Rory so much.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14940629706498630071" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_447702407" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/447702407" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/447702407?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer447702407" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11886421525511597646"><b> Just like with the first two, this book is another gem of a fluff read. A lighthearted, sexy, hilarious, over-the-top frenemies-to-lovers story. Pure fun! </b><br/><br/>Teasing, banter, a cocoa addiction, a bad boy, a tough girl and some seriously crazy pranks involving super glued boxer shorts, three week old fermented yogurt, laxatives, being hog tied with medical tape, being chained to a toilet, many purple nurples…. the list goes on to ‘fun’ that landed them more than a few overnight jail time and bans f</span>
  <span id="freeText11886421525511597646" style="display:none"><b> Just like with the first two, this book is another gem of a fluff read. A lighthearted, sexy, hilarious, over-the-top frenemies-to-lovers story. Pure fun! </b><br><br>Teasing, banter, a cocoa addiction, a bad boy, a tough girl and some seriously crazy pranks involving super glued boxer shorts, three week old fermented yogurt, laxatives, being hog tied with medical tape, being chained to a toilet, many purple nurples…. the list goes on to ‘fun’ that landed them more than a few overnight jail time and bans from stores :P<br><br>Guys, don’t take this book seriously, just enjoy the ride :-&gt;<br><br>Ever since preschool Connor has been certain that Rory “had been put on this earth solely for him to torture and torture her he did.” He would tease her mercilessless and she’s give back every bit as good as she got. As they grew older, the severity and frequence of their pranks grew until pretty much everyone in the town knew to duck for cover when they were breathing the same air.<br><br><i> “She’d been the prettiest little girl that he’d ever seen and he just had to push her and pull on her pigtails.” </i> <br><br>Now, twenty-five years since they first met in preschool, their two rival construction companies have been hired to do a joint project much to the disgruntlement of both Rory and Connor, and are they are forced not only to work together but to collaborate on the job, the constant close quarters lead them to explore if maybe there is something other than just the intense desire to torture each other between them.<br><br><i> <b> “As long as I’m stuck with you on this project and you try to get in my way, anything goes,” she said…<br>“Is that a fact?” he demanded evenly.<br>“Yes,” she practically hissed as her eyes narrowed no his.<br>You’re only here because of my generosity, Rory. Push me and you might just find yourself locked in the trunk of a car and on a ferry headed off to Nova Scotia… again,” he said softly, loving the way she practically shook with rage against him.<br>“I knew that was you, you bastard!” she snarled…<br>“You deserved it,” he felt obligated to remind her. </b></i> <br><br>Oh Connor *shakes head* … lol, I had to laugh at his antics. He was just such a lovable asshat. On one had it was totally cute that he secretly cared for her, but when you got inside his head, I just couldn’t wait for the next time Rory would kick his ass.<br><br>But I loved that no matter what Connor did, Rory never gave him the satisfaction of ‘winning’ and always stood up for herself. Oh, and lets not forget that she’s got five hot older brothers watching her back too (hmmm… *wonders about future books*)<br><br>And I was not expecting the HOTNESS from this book! Their first love scene took up 4% of my kindle!! Whew *fans self*<br><br><i> “Oh my God!” A woman whispered loudly. “They’re going to do it on the front lawn!” </i> <br><br>And in case you are missing those yummy, always-hungry Bradford men from the first two books, fear not! Both Jason and Trevor have absolutely hilarious cameos that had me laughing myself silly! Love those guys so much &lt;3<br><br><i> “Tell me that you didn’t break the ban, Rory. Tell me that there aren’t two Bradfords beating the shit out of each other over the last slice of cheese in my kitchen,” he pleaded, already knowing and dreading the answer.” </i><br><br>I did like also that as strange as their relationship was, when the inevitable ‘something’ came between them, it was dealt with rationally and functionally instead of the usual freak out and stupidity that often plagues novels.<br><br>And despite the craziness of the story, I did love that there was a touch of sweet heart warming backstory that came out that gave a whole new insight into Connor. It was<br><br><i> <b> “When this project was over, he was keeping her, deal or no deal. She belonged with him…This morning he had a taste of what it could be like between them and he’d have to be out of his fucking mind to give that up.” </b></i> <br><br>I can’t wait for more from this series!!<br><br>Now, if you’ll excuse me, I’m feeling a massive craving for some hot cocoa :D<br><br>CASTING:<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396387i/764026._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="11886421525511597646" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

When i found out at the beginning of this year that R.L. was writing the third book in the Neighbor from Hell series, i died. <div id="review_625389948" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Jennifer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4482512-jennifer"><img alt="Jennifer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1374781588p2/4482512.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/625389948?book_show_action=true">May 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer" href="/user/show/4482512-jennifer">Jennifer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4482512-jennifer?shelf=jerks">jerks</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer625389948" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16309646666953016659"><b>4 HOT COCOA STARS!!!!</b><br/><br/><b>FUN.</b><br/><br/>Love should be fun.<br/><br/>And that is exactly what this book is. <b>LOVE and FUN.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423043i/842508._SX540_.jpg' alt='Big Girls Don't Cry They Get Even Necklace' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Ever since they were little, Rory and Connor have hated each with a <b>vengeance.</b> The pranks and fights were never-ending. There was always a constant battle between the two of them, so much so that the whole town knew to stay away from them. If they walked into a room together, people would flee. But they can’t seem to stay away from each other because <b>they secretly love to torture the other.</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>They say</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText16309646666953016659" style="display:none"><b>4 HOT COCOA STARS!!!!</b><br><br><b>FUN.</b><br><br>Love should be fun.<br><br>And that is exactly what this book is. <b>LOVE and FUN.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423043i/842508._SX540_.jpg" alt="Big Girls Don't Cry They Get Even Necklace" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ever since they were little, Rory and Connor have hated each with a <b>vengeance.</b> The pranks and fights were never-ending. There was always a constant battle between the two of them, so much so that the whole town knew to stay away from them. If they walked into a room together, people would flee. But they can’t seem to stay away from each other because <b>they secretly love to torture the other.</b><br><br><b>
  <i>They say there’s a fine line between love and hate…</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423043i/842509._SX540_.jpg" alt="Love Hate" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>He might be a life ruining bastard, but he was a hot life ruining bastard and her poor neglected body didn’t realize that it should hate him as much as her heart and brain did.</i>
</b><br><br><b>My Connor:</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423043i/842510._SY540_.jpg" alt="Reynaldo Gianecchini (Brazil - actor)" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>It figured that the one man that treated her like a woman was the one that made her wish she was a man so that she could kick his ass.</i>
</b><br><br><b>My Rory:</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423043i/842511._SY540_.jpg" alt="blond" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Finally, they are forced to work together on a project, and as you can guess, the sparks start to fly. Of course, the pranks keeps going, which makes for a <b>hilarious book!!!</b><br><br>Their relationship is perfect because they started off as frenemies (friends/enemies). Love/hate relationships are the best. It means there’s <b>PASSION.</b> <br><br><b>
  <i>“As long as you remember that I hate you,” Rory mumbled against his lips.<br>“I’ll remember,” he promised.<br>“And you hate me,” she reminded him as she continued to caress his lips with light, teasing kisses that had his arms tightening around her and his body trembling with the need to consumer her.<br>“With a passon.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423043i/842512.jpg" alt="Lots of cute ideas for couple's pictures :)" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423043i/842513._SY540_.jpg" alt=" " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423043i/842514.jpg" alt="together." class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love me some drama in books, but I really don’t care for it in real life. So this book is perfect for a <b>light-hearted feel-good laugh-your-ass-off love and fun.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423043i/842515.jpg" alt="Best part of my day" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423043i/842516._SY540_.jpg" alt="Love Bakes Good Cakes: Drink Coffee or Hot Cocoa printable (8x10)" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Loved that ending!!! It was one of my favorite and most memorable parts of the book!!!</b><br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_676240776" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/676240776" />
    <a title="Runell" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2824698-runell"><img alt="Runell" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1541892887p2/2824698.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/676240776?book_show_action=true">Jul 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Runell" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Runell" href="/user/show/2824698-runell">Runell</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780988573208" href="/book/show/18776101-checkmate">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Runell by: </span>
      Elizabeth
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2824698-runell?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2824698-runell?shelf=onmykindle">onmykindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2824698-runell?shelf=femaleauthors">femaleauthors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2824698-runell?shelf=adultromance">adultromance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2824698-runell?shelf=enemiestolovers">enemiestolovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2824698-runell?shelf=1star">1star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2824698-runell?shelf=multiplepovs">multiplepovs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2824698-runell?shelf=adultcontemporary">adultcontemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer676240776" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12789088937140777397">To say that I was disappointed with this book would be my first understatement of 2014.<br/><br/>After having read the first two books, which I absolutely loved, I was <i>sure</i> that <i>Checkmate</i> would be the same. <br/><br/>It wasn't. At all.<br/><br/>To say that Connor and Rory annoyed the ever-loving shit out of me would be my second understatement of 2014. Connor, to me, was a chauvinistic ass. Yes, I understand that the entire time he was in love with Rory and that he didn't want her to get hurt and that he wanted everyone to t</span>
  <span id="freeText12789088937140777397" style="display:none">To say that I was disappointed with this book would be my first understatement of 2014.<br><br>After having read the first two books, which I absolutely loved, I was <i>sure</i> that <i>Checkmate</i> would be the same. <br><br>It wasn't. At all.<br><br>To say that Connor and Rory annoyed the ever-loving shit out of me would be my second understatement of 2014. Connor, to me, was a chauvinistic ass. Yes, I understand that the entire time he was in love with Rory and that he didn't want her to get hurt and that he wanted everyone to treat her like the woman she is and not just like one of the guys, but damn it all to hell, when did "fetching his drinks, being at his beck and call" become two of the qualifications of being a woman? Last time I checked, even though I don't "fetch" any man his drink like a dog "fetching" a stick, nor am I at at any man's "beck and call" like I don't have anything better to do in any given day of my life, I still have the parts that make me a woman. Huh. It must be a medical miracle.<br><br>Oh, Connor, you poor misguided fool.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382639558ra/6085793.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now, I like hot chocolate. In fact, I love it (I don't drink coffee, so there you go). However, after having the word "cocoa" mentioned in some fashion because Rory is such a "little addict" over a hundred times (oh yeah, I did a search on the word and it popped up over a hundred times), all I wanted to do was say:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381206551ra/4526170.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I get that Connor and Rory's antics were supposed to be funny--The key word there? <i>Supposed</i>. What they actually were? Annoying and juvenile. I didn't laugh a single time until I hit the 64% mark and Jason and Trevor, the characters from the previous two books whom I absolutely loved, made an appearance. <i>Then</i>, I laughed, and laughed hard, which is what I should have been doing the entire time over the course of me reading this book.<br><br>And then when Connor comes up with his master plan to snatch Rory's brothers away from her and run her out of business, but then in the process ends up realizing that those feelings that he had thought he had gotten over when he was a teenager and that he still really loved her? Yeah, that's when the book took a sharp turn from silly to outright asinine. <br><br>I can see why so many people loved this book, honestly I can, so I will concede to the idea that maybe it was just me.<br><br>Maybe.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12789088937140777397" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Didn't live up to the first 2 in the series! </b><br/><br/>I love this series, but this book didn't quite work for me like <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11381643.Playing_for_Keeps__Neighbor_from_Hell___1_' title='Playing for Keeps (Neighbor from Hell, #1) by R.L.   <span id="freeText6749449112382597623" style="display:none"><br /><b>3 Stars! Didn't live up to the first 2 in the series! </b><br /><br />I love this series, but this book didn't quite work for me like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11381643.Playing_for_Keeps__Neighbor_from_Hell___1_" title="Playing for Keeps (Neighbor from Hell, #1) by R.L. Mathewson" rel="nofollow noopener">Playing for Keeps</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12351649.Perfection__Neighbor_from_Hell___2_" title="Perfection (Neighbor from Hell, #2) by R.L. Yes, it was funny at times, but where the other two books moved forward at a nice pace, this went round and round. Maybe it was because Connor and Rory were childhood nemesis and getting to their relationship seemed endless to me, lots of reminiscing. I also thought some of their revenge tactics were over the top, and bordered on mean. On the plus side, Jason and Trevor made an appearance...love those Bradfords! It was also a fairly steamy read, something the author is good a writing, she doesn't skim on the heat. <br /><br />Overall, some fun, but a little boring! Even though this one was a little off for me, I'm looking forward to reading, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17352874.Truce_The_Historic_Neighbor_from_Hell__Neighbor_from_Hell___4_" title="Truce The Historic Neighbor from Hell (Neighbor from Hell, #4) by R.L. <div id="review_1494047474" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1494047474" />
    <a title="Naksed" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/29458352-naksed"><img alt="Naksed" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417804998p2/29458352.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1494047474?book_show_action=true">Jan 03, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Naksed" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Naksed" href="/user/show/29458352-naksed">Naksed</a>
      </span>

          marked it as dnf




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29458352-naksed?shelf=bully-romance">bully-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29458352-naksed?shelf=annoying-heroine">annoying-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29458352-naksed?shelf=hot-mess">hot-mess</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29458352-naksed?shelf=hero-is-a-big-fat-jerk">hero-is-a-big-fat-jerk</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1494047474" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4387816817468324794">I am ambivalent towards "bully romances" because I was victimized by a bully or two in childhood, and that stuff really leaves indelible marks on you even when you leave it far, far, behind, and also I don't like the message it gives to young girls, that the big fat jerk abusing you really really really deep down actually likes you, so it's on you that he is acting this way. <br/><br/>Some bully romances that dealt with the topic realistically and sensitively, and showcased true remorse and a fair bit of </span>
  <span id="freeText4387816817468324794" style="display:none">I am ambivalent towards "bully romances" because I was victimized by a bully or two in childhood, and that stuff really leaves indelible marks on you even when you leave it far, far, behind, and also I don't like the message it gives to young girls, that the big fat jerk abusing you really really really deep down actually likes you, so it's on you that he is acting this way. <br /><br />Some bully romances that dealt with the topic realistically and sensitively, and showcased true remorse and a fair bit of groveling from the former bully, I have enjoyed, true. Nevertheless, this trope is certainly not my favorite when it comes to romances.<br /><br />In <i>Checkmate</i>, at least in the first half of it before I DNF, though both protags engage in this sick game of one-upping each other, it is very clear that the male character has always been and continues to be the instigator. Not only that but he actually enjoys the hell out of it and even justifies it because in his view, he is not inflicting permanent damage and he is actually "saving" her from would-be boyfriends who are not worthy of her. This delusional crap started with him when they were in preschool and has continued to escalate in their thirties. Two professional business owners are playing rough pranks on each other, being disrespectful, mean, and physically inappropriate while tackling an important project? And their friends and families standing by doing nothing, not to mention an entire town that uses their feud as entertainment? <br /><br />It was just too over the top and implausible for me to suspend my disbelief. Plus it seemed like a lame copy of that French film Jeux d'enfants, starring Marion Cotillard, where the couple similarly engage in progressively more outlandish and violent pranks from the time they are children to their inevitable demise as adults. I disliked that film for its cruelty and darkness and I did not like it reinvented in a supposedly fluffy American romance book either. Just could not stomach the horrible male protagonist who sounds more like a deranged, dangerous stalker and an annoying heroine who spends more time making hot chocolate than an houseful of Santa's elves.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4387816817468324794" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/785079341?book_show_action=true">Dec 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake">Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer785079341" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7197256288477282292">I enjoyed the first two in this series, but Mathewson lost me on this one with the behavior of Connor, Rory, and the whole town really. I am all for over the top behavior and cliches (I am a romance fan after all), however, I just don't buy that two people would act this way--and more startlingly-- that an entire town would simply accept two people acting this way.<br/><br/> </span>

          </span>

<div id="review_402283473" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/402283473" />
    <a title="Kennedy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10738375-kennedy"><img alt="Kennedy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1341599011p2/10738375.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/402283473?book_show_action=true">Aug 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kennedy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kennedy" href="/user/show/10738375-kennedy">Kennedy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer402283473&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer402283473" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16839333936619425567">I am so addicted to the Bradfords and how funny their food obsession is that I'm having a hard time not being disappointed in knowing who the main characters are in this novel. I'm still very excited for it to come out and to read it but please, please let it be as funny and if you possibly can please bring back the Bradfords! I miss them. In the meantime I will need to read more Mathewson books to see if I enjoy them as much as I have this series. If you are deciding whether to jump in or not, </span>
  <span id="freeText16839333936619425567" style="display:none">I am so addicted to the Bradfords and how funny their food obsession is that I'm having a hard time not being disappointed in knowing who the main characters are in this novel. I'm still very excited for it to come out and to read it but please, please let it be as funny and if you possibly can please bring back the Bradfords! I miss them. In the meantime I will need to read more Mathewson books to see if I enjoy them as much as I have this series. If you are deciding whether to jump in or not, jump in already. <br /><br />Ok, so the Bradford’s are in this book but it’s not quite the same for me and not as funny. I didn’t have any moments where I laughed out loud. That being said, I still enjoyed the book. I like the way that Mathewson writes and the characters she creates. You have to love all of the handsome, big, strong, protective, useful, reliable and yet annoying male characters she has running around everywhere. And I like the way they fall in love. It reminds me of the werewolves imprinting in Twilight – once they are in love they have eyes only for the one girl and would do anything for her. It’s fictional of course, but still fun. We meet Connor and Rory in this story. They have known each other since kindergarten and spend time every day making each other’s lives beyond difficult. They have competing businesses and even live right next door to each other. Connor has known for awhile that he is in love with Rory but believes that he lost his chance at being hers awhile ago so his mission is to constantly annoy her, yet if anyone else is anything less than perfect to her he has something to say (or do) about it. While working on a project together Conner proposes a deal where Rory is supposed to pretend to be his loving girlfriend in exchange for building a set of attic suites that she dreamed up for the current remodel. They fall in love and end up together which is exactly the way I like it. The path is fun with just enough minor twists and turns and some interesting stops along the way. Thrown into the mix is Conner’s high school friend who is battling leukemia yet doesn’t want anyone to know and doesn’t want the required treatment. Rory ends up secretly donating bone marrow that helps him to recover. The actual love story and how the characters interact is much like the previous two in the series but I still enjoy the story and will continue to seek out the author. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16839333936619425567" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_412668792" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/412668792" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/412668792?book_show_action=true">Sep 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer412668792" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2219775421725566750">God, I love this series! I love it when you can pick up a book and, before you even open it, know what you can expect, and know that it’s going to be a great read. The Neighbour from Hell books are like that - fun, light, swoony and sexy, and utterly, utterly hilarious!<br/><br/>Rory and Connor are absolutely dynamite! They live to torment each other. Ever since preschool they have been at each other with pranks, jokes, teasing and embarrassing the hell out of each other. Their antics have resulted in jai</span>
  <span id="freeText2219775421725566750" style="display:none">God, I love this series! I love it when you can pick up a book and, before you even open it, know what you can expect, and know that it’s going to be a great read. The Neighbour from Hell books are like that - fun, light, swoony and sexy, and utterly, utterly hilarious!<br /><br />Rory and Connor are absolutely dynamite! They live to torment each other. Ever since preschool they have been at each other with pranks, jokes, teasing and embarrassing the hell out of each other. Their antics have resulted in jail stays, restaurant and grocery store bans, and a situation where whenever they are in the same room, people run and hide. Little titbits of their childhood together and all of the things they did to each other are revealed throughout the story, and it’s absolutely freaking hilarious! <br /><br />Now they are all grown up, both of them strong, confident and stubborn, and still torturing each other – sometimes it's hilarious, sometimes it's totally cringe worthy (but mostly it's hilarious). <br /><br /><i>“All that mattered was that he could look forward to aggravating the piss out of Rory each and every night.” </i><br /><br />But when they are forced to work together, things, unsurprisingly, start to change and the fire between them becomes something completely different as they find themselves overwhelmingly attracted to each other. The two of them fight their attraction so hard, and watching them try to rationalise it is so freaking funny. But when they eventually cave… HOLY FREAKING HOTNESS, these two have some SERIOUS chemistry! My kindle was steaming!<br /><br />But it’s not all sex, there is some very deep emotion going on too, and watching Rory and Connor come to realise their feelings, and then seeing Connor, in particular, just go with it and put himself out there, was brilliant. I will admit that Connor’s motives for his ‘big plan’ were pretty deplorable, but I totally forgave him while watching him come to realise exactly what Rory meant to him. And from that point on the poor girl had no chance, because he was never going to let her go! And through it all he treated her like a Princess – something she had never experienced before, and I loved him for it! And damn, the man can bring the swoon! <br /><br /><i>“I want you, Rory,” he said against her lips. “Forever.” <br />“I want you too, Connor,” ...<br />“You’ve got me”</i><br /><br />And when we are given even more insight into their past history, and realise exactly what had been going on, and for how long, and how much of an impact these two have unknowingly had over each other’s lives for all of these years, it makes their coming together even sweeter!<br /><br />In other happy news - Jason and Trevor are back (Rory is a cousin to the Bradford family) – and starving of course, and they are just as fantastic as always. I was laughing pretty much from the moment they appeared on the page. God, I love those boys!<br /><br /><i>“Oh my God! Stop eating that!” <br />“Your trail mix tastes funny,” Trevor said with a cringe. <br />“That wasn’t trail mix, you bastard! That was potpourri!” <br />“Well, that explains a lot,” he said, giving her a sheepish smile as he returned the large wooden bowl back to the side table. She didn’t need to look to know that he’d already eaten half the bowl of potpourri. She didn’t even bother asking him what the hell was wrong with him since she knew the answer. <br />The man was a Bradford. <br />Enough said.</i><br /><br />And when you add into the mix Rory’s five gorgeously protective older brothers, and the entire Bradford clan at a family reunion, that’s a lot of Alpha male roaming around! And their reactions to the unfolding romance are priceless. <br /><br />I loved both Rory and Connor, and their story. I hope that R.L. Mathewson continues on with this series, because these books are just pure win :)<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2219775421725566750" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="A_Ryan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23384676-a-ryan"><img alt="A_Ryan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1408592469p2/23384676.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1001375631?book_show_action=true">Jul 20, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="A_Ryan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="A_Ryan" href="/user/show/23384676-a-ryan">A_Ryan</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1001375631" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5635094561154827714"><b> 5 TOTALLY BRILLIANT LIFE RUINING BASTARD STARS!!!!!!<br/><br/>UPDATED REVIEW AFTER RE-READING </b><br/><br/><b> Synopsis: </b> Enemies since the age of five, when he first pushed her off the swing and pulled on her pigtails, Connor and Rory have become notorious for their passionate antics throughout their local town. But a new business deal has forced them to work side by side, and now the power plays, mind games and the constant bickering only add fuel to the growing fire between them and their unavoidable pull towards eac</span>
  <span id="freeText5635094561154827714" style="display:none"><b> 5 TOTALLY BRILLIANT LIFE RUINING BASTARD STARS!!!!!!<br /><br />UPDATED REVIEW AFTER RE-READING </b><br /><br /><b> Synopsis: </b> Enemies since the age of five, when he first pushed her off the swing and pulled on her pigtails, Connor and Rory have become notorious for their passionate antics throughout their local town. But a new business deal has forced them to work side by side, and now the power plays, mind games and the constant bickering only add fuel to the growing fire between them and their unavoidable pull towards each other. <br /><br /><b> Best Bit: </b> I loved the two main characters! Connor is certainly one of my favourite heroes... I especially love how he deludes himself with his dream of having Rory one day becoming HIS secretary, (bringing him coffee in tight fitting clothes). His daydreams are seriously hilarious. And so much more enjoyable to read because it's obvious that he loves Rory so much and in reality he is just putty in her hands. <br /><br />Rory is one tough and independent heroine though, and had spent her life as 'just one of the boys' (thanks in large part to growing up with five older brothers) but Connor still sees her as "feminine" and when he's not totally "ruining her life", he treats her like a real lady (...he also beats the crap out of anyone and everyone who doesn't treat her with total respect...but he does it all without her even knowing.)<br /><br />Also, RL Mathewson's writing is easy, no-nonsense and dripping with humour on every page. R.L Mathewson inserts some of the best humour into her books, and I think she had some great fun thinking up of all the wonderful pranks Rory and Connor played on each other over the years. Each one was funnier than the last! I loved the prologue, which outlines a lot of the pranks that take place throughout their childhood, adolescence and college; and later the moments when they are forced to share a pizza (by which I mean they're unable to allow eachother even one slice of pizza-glory and keep grabbing the one slice off one another mid-bite), or when they enter a restaurant (from which they've been banned due to previous antics) while everyone stops and stares and updates their twitter feed, or when the cousins arrive like food-craving zombies. .. all these moments (and more) were slightly ridiculous but utterly entertaining!!<br /><br /><br /><b> Worst bit: </b> I totally love this series and have bought all the books. I'm about to start on her historical romance...and can't wait. However, the writing style is simple, and the editing is poor, but the story (and the fun) more than make up for it!<br /><br /><b> Recommended for: </b> Lovers of enemies-to-lovers romance. This one is totally fun and very low on the angst. A bonus for fans of the series are the cameo appearances by Jason &amp; Haley (from #1) and Trevor and Zoe (from #2) but you don't need to read the previous books in the series to enjoy this one.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5635094561154827714" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

<span id="freeTextContainer8275371281534507167"><b>He never gave up this easily,never. Not even when they were fourteen and she may have pantsed him in front of the entire school one afternoon and he may have broken his arm in an attempt to pull her out of the air duct where she might have been hiding.He simply waited until the cast was dry and his mother was looking the other way before he snuck out of the exam room at the clinic over on Chestnut and made his way to the waiting room where he knew her father would make her wait so that she could</b></span>
  <span id="freeText8275371281534507167" style="display:none"><b>He never gave up this easily,never. Not even when they were fourteen and she may have pantsed him in front of the entire school one afternoon and he may have broken his arm in an attempt to pull her out of the air duct where she might have been hiding.He simply waited until the cast was dry and his mother was looking the other way before he snuck out of the exam room at the clinic over on Chestnut and made his way to the waiting room where he knew her father would make her wait so that she could give him the customary muttered"sorry." <br /><br />As soon as Connor stepped into the waiting room she knew that she was in deep shit. She'd barely turned to run and hide when he clamped his good hand around her wrist and dragged her kicking and screaming into the staff kitchenette where he found a strawberry yogurt three years past its expiration date in the back of the fridge. For the next ten minutes he sat on her back while he forced her to eat the brown concoction and even when the doctor, three nurses and his mother tried to drag him off of her,he still managed to shove a large spoonful of the fuzzy gunk into her mouth.</b><br /><br />That's pretty much how life was for Connor and Rory. Connor made her life a living hell and she always paid him back. That's been happening for 25 years and got them banned from 57 places(see their first "date"). It's is one of the things I liked the most in this book.<br /><br /><b>LRJ</b>Remember that.Connor has it as a tattoo and there is a lot of history behind these letters.<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ To be honest I didn't cross my mind that Connor was in love with her as a teenager.I thought he later developed his feelings for her. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>Still I won't spoil the meaning of the 3 letters.<br /><br /><b>“My baking isn’t that bad!” Zoe argued.<br />“Sweetie," Rory said, pausing in her search to reach over and give Zoe’s hand a quick squeeze,“there isn’t a Bradford alive that will willingly touch your baked goods.”<br />“I overheard Jason and Trevor telling everyone that you baked my cupcakes so that they wouldn’t have to share,”Haley added softly as she took Zoe’s other hand into hers.“Not one single Bradford will touch them.In fact,they actually demanded that everything the guys claimed that you baked be taken away and given its own section.”</b><br /><br />If the book was a TV show it would be like: Starring Connor O’Neil and Rory James. Special guest stars Jason,Hayley, Trevor and Zoe plus for a quick appearance the newborn (they get born in the book) twins of Trevor and Zoe. I don't think I would have given 5 stars if at least one character of them wasn't in this book.<b>She didn’t even bother asking him what the hell was wrong with him since she knew the answer. The man was a Bradford.Enough said.</b>Plus I missed Jason and Trevor's Bradford appetite. Did you know that if a Bradford showed his pretty face at the city when our couple lives they would get to spend a night in jail, pay 2,000$ and do community service? Here are some quotes about that appetite;<br /><br /><b>
  <i>Even though he’d never met them before,he knew that they were Bradfords.The tales of the other side of Rory’s family were well known.They were often used to scare little children into behaving.If they didn’t,they knew the Bradfords would come and eat them.<i><b><br /><br />You are only allowed to hit each sample cart ten times and that’s it.”<br />“You bitch!” Trevor and Jason gasped in outrage.Ignoring them,she continued.“And while we’re at it,let’s get to the other rules.”<br />“Rules?”Trevor repeated slowly,his eyes narrowing to slits on her.<br />“You are not allowed to eat in any of the restaurants in town or within twenty miles of the town unless I am there with you.”At that announcement,Jason’s eyes narrowed on her,too.“Also,you are not to buy anything that requires you to show your driver’s license.If you hit the grocery store,you’re each limited to one carriage full.You can order in,but you’re only allowed to order enough for six people.”<br />“I’ve always hated you,”Jason bit out in a huff as he turned his back on her and headed for the double doors of the warehouse.<br />“Ditto"Trevor said.<br /><br />"Tell me that you didn’t break the ban,Rory.Tell me that there aren’t two Bradfords beating the shit out of each other over the last slice of cheese in my kitchen"<br /><br />“That wasn’t trail mix, you bastard!<u>That was potpourri!</u>”<br /><br />As much as she'd love to dismiss the possibility,and she would have if it had been anyone else,but this was a Bradford that she was dealing with here so she had to ask,"You didn't eat my box of baking soda,did you?"</b><br /><br />Closing (not that I said much)I liked this book but less than the first two. In some parts is better but it lacks in others. Connor and Rory are different than the other 2 couples. The book made me laugh and left me wanting for a 4th book.<br /><br />"I probably should remind you that your brothers said that they wouldn't bail you out of jail again for the next three years after what happened the last time and that if you kill him then you'll probably lose this contract"</i></i>
</b></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/79648381-mg-bury-me-with-my-kindle-a-really-long-charger?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/79648381-mg-bury-me-with-my-kindle-a-really-long-charger?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/79648381-mg-bury-me-with-my-kindle-a-really-long-charger?shelf=second-chance">second-chance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/79648381-mg-bury-me-with-my-kindle-a-really-long-charger?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/79648381-mg-bury-me-with-my-kindle-a-really-long-charger?shelf=lets-make-a-deal">lets-make-a-deal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/79648381-mg-bury-me-with-my-kindle-a-really-long-charger?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/79648381-mg-bury-me-with-my-kindle-a-really-long-charger?shelf=fake-relationship">fake-relationship</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/79648381-mg-bury-me-with-my-kindle-a-really-long-charger?shelf=humorous">humorous</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/79648381-mg-bury-me-with-my-kindle-a-really-long-charger?shelf=enemies-to-lovers">enemies-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/79648381-mg-bury-me-with-my-kindle-a-really-long-charger?shelf=workplace-shenanigans">workplace-shenanigans</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2994282135" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer666902197490540536"><b>4 enemies-to-lovers done right stars</b><br/><br/>So far, this 3rd book of the series is my favorite. Book 1 was good but had too much unnecessary angst (porridge was too hot); Book 2 had some whiny mcs (too cold); but this one has baby bear written all over it. Though this is part of a series and some characters recur, it may be preferred but is not necessary to have read the previous books in the series to enjoy this one.<br/><br/>Rory James refers to her neighbor and life long nemesis Connor O'Neil as "life-ruiner."</span>
  <span id="freeText666902197490540536" style="display:none"><b>4 enemies-to-lovers done right stars</b><br /><br />So far, this 3rd book of the series is my favorite. Book 1 was good but had too much unnecessary angst (porridge was too hot); Book 2 had some whiny mcs (too cold); but this one has baby bear written all over it. Though this is part of a series and some characters recur, it may be preferred but is not necessary to have read the previous books in the series to enjoy this one.<br /><br />Rory James refers to her neighbor and life long nemesis Connor O'Neil as "life-ruiner." Every problem she has traces back to that jerk who has pulled her pigtails since day 1 on the playground, landed her in detention throughout school, and had her banned from many restaurants and stores in their small town for years. But don't feel badly for her because she has given as good as she has gotten as Connor was in detention with her, is also banned from many establishments, and was once her cellmate in prison (an event alluded to a couple of times as the reason for Rory's life-ruinage, but isn't fully explained until much later into the story). The a-hole even bought the house next to hers just to continue his daily torments! And now, as she is running late, guess who steals the parking spot she has been patiently waiting on with her turn signal flashing and then tells her he's happy to move it --- after his meeting! Rory is already infuriated... imagine her reaction when the construction and renovation project they both put bids in on has had its timeline significantly shortened so the client asks them BOTH to work on it in order to get it completed in time!! Impossible. No way the two who cannot be in each other's presence can go 1 minute without pranking the other can possibly work together on a career-making deal like this one.<br /><br />While Rory believes Connor to be her life ruiner, Connor finds Rory to be the best part of his day. He has even "saved" her a few times (without her knowing, of course!) when he felt her 5 older brothers weren't doing their job effectively in protecting her. He loves that she never backs down from him, doesn't cry "like a girl," and gives as good as she gets. And the fact that she is the most beautiful woman he has ever seen doesn't hurt either. But he knows that she doesn't feel anything for him, so there isn't any chance for the two of them to have a future. Although... what if he can get her to play along as his doting gf by promising her something she can't resist: her dream renovation? Maybe he can have his cake and eat it too. But what happens when they realize that their tempers aren't the only thing that goes "boom" in each other's presence? Is there any way a "temporary" deal can be made permanent? <br /><br />What I liked:<br />--- Very little unnecessary angst (and when there was some, it was resolved quickly)<br />--- Likeable main characters with humorous interactions<br />--- Revisiting some of the characters from earlier books (the James and Bradford families are cousins)<br />--- Steamy goodness<br /><br />What I didn't like as much:<br />--- There was some childish stuff happening when they were supposedly adults, and a time or two it seemed to go too far<br />--- Seemed silly that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Connor didn't feel he could tell the woman he was in love with and whom was also his business partner about what was happening with his best friend who was also one of the employees on the project - I get the "bestie" secrets aspect, but at that point, it just seemed silly not to share pertinent info until so late, especially since the friend was believed to be lazy and "hung over" all the time when he was really very ill <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Overall, a good read with likeable main characters, an interesting plot, steamy goodness, and a low reading on the relationship angst aspect! <br /><br />Plot --- 4/5<br />Main Characters --- 4/5<br />Supporting Cast --- 4/5<br />Steam Level* --- 3.5/5<br />Violence --- some (there is a description of something that happened in the past, but not graphic)<br />Language --- they're on a construction site, so curse words happen<br />POV --- 3rd<br /><br />*Note that steam level is not a rating so much as a how hot was it: 0/5 - clean; 1/5 - mild; 2/5 - sensual but nothing descriptive; 3/5 - now we're getting somewhere; 4/5 - yes please! ; 5/5 - they did EVERYTHING in this one, y'all</span>
  <a data-text-id="666902197490540536" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_324187286" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/324187286" />
    <a title="Keri" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2335749-keri"><img alt="Keri" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1373210138p2/2335749.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/324187286?book_show_action=true">May 05, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Keri" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Keri" href="/user/show/2335749-keri">Keri</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2335749-keri?shelf=e-book">e-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2335749-keri?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2335749-keri?shelf=romance-contemporary">romance-contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2335749-keri?shelf=2010s-read">2010s-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer324187286" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10587564391260798782">It was pretty good. Rory and Connor have tortured each other since grade school, to the point that they have been banned from being seen together in several places in their town. But since they have houses right next to each other, they can torture each other with impunity and they do. Now they are vying for the same construction jobs. Surprisingly they have both been giving a contract to finish a hotel in 5 months and gain a bonus. But Connor has nefarious plans to take Rory's men, the contract</span>
  <span id="freeText10587564391260798782" style="display:none">It was pretty good. Rory and Connor have tortured each other since grade school, to the point that they have been banned from being seen together in several places in their town. But since they have houses right next to each other, they can torture each other with impunity and they do. Now they are vying for the same construction jobs. Surprisingly they have both been giving a contract to finish a hotel in 5 months and gain a bonus. But Connor has nefarious plans to take Rory's men, the contract and Rory herself. This was a fun romp and the things that Rory and Connor do to one another was funny at first, but it got old fast. <br /><br />Connor figures out a way to have Rory pretend to be his girlfriend and then into his bed where he always wanted her. It was a case of he had a crush on her as a kid, so he pulled her hair, only he and her got stuck in that groove and the one time he tried to get out of it, it ended in disaster. Now Rory says that Connor ruined her life at 18 and he felt like he had too. Once we got the real story, I still couldn't figure out how he "ruined" her life. She was an extremely successful businesswoman in a man's world, because of that incident. How was her life ruined? We also get to see Jason and Trevor and their ladies, as the Bradfords are cousins to Rory and her brothers. Their were moments of seriousness as we find out what Andrew is dealing with and how Connor is struggling with his friend's decision. The steam factor was high with Rory and Connor once they put their hostilities behind them and find the love they had both been hiding for each other. I get Rory's hot chocolate addiction. *sigh* </span>
  <a data-text-id="10587564391260798782" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ekKIZT3L8mAmR4JeMsylorNVuMvHacjenMRv6ybHYUWakDJL7GYYO5BZmRwOZ2MwXAaXi7/hqOFBviHtln0v8w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('daAw21wxHCqyjx/e0+em7euKjoBs2cCBfmt25SjL73mVcor1jZz2cQSRBJzvTGB/BNmhwBRRoL6jETjjmHGhzw==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer5137059539228016937">New York Times Bestselling author, R.L. Mathewson was born in Massachusetts. She’s known for her humor, quick wit and ability to write relatable characters. She currently has several paranormal and contemporary romance series published including the Neighbor from Hell series. <br/><br/>Growing up, R.L. Mathewson was a painfully shy bookworm. After high school she attended college, worked as a bellhop, fast </span>
  <span id="freeText5137059539228016937" style="display:none">New York Times Bestselling author, R.L. Mathewson was born in Massachusetts. She’s known for her humor, quick wit and ability to write relatable characters. She currently has several paranormal and contemporary romance series published including the Neighbor from Hell series. <br /><br />Growing up, R.L. Mathewson was a painfully shy bookworm. After high school she attended college, worked as a bellhop, fast food cook, and a museum worker until she decided to take an EMT course. Working as an EMT helped her get over her shyness as well as left her with some fond memories and some rather disturbing ones that from time to time show up in one of her books. <br /><br />Today, R.L. Mathewson is the single mother of two children that keep her on her toes. She has a bit of a romance novel addiction as well as a major hot chocolate addiction and on a perfect day, she combines the two. <br /><br />In 2019/2020, R.L. Mathewson will be publishing Devastated, the first Anger Management novel, Tall, Dark &amp; Furious, the 6th installment to the Pyte/Sentinel series, Irresistible, the long anticipated novel for the Neighbor from Hell Series as well as many more books throughout the year, paranormals, contemporaries, and YAs. </span>
